<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trends_since_2000">Trends since 2000</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Tourism&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Trends since 2000">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_(cropped).JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3520" data-file-width="2585" decoding="async" height="191" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG/140px-AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG/210px-AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG/280px-AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_%28cropped%29.JPG 2x" width="140"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AYRIVANK_MONASTERY_103_(cropped).JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Cultural_tourism" title="Cultural tourism">Cultural tourism</a>: tourists outside a <a href="/wiki/Geghard" title="Geghard">Geghard</a> monastery in <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, 2015</div></div></div>
<p>As a result of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Late-2000s_recession" title="Late-2000s recession">late-2000s recession</a>, international arrivals experienced a strong slowdown beginning in June 2008. Growth from 2007 to 2008 was only 3.7% during the first eight months of 2008. This slowdown on international tourism demand was also reflected in the air transport industry, with negative growth in September 2008 and a 3.3% growth in passenger traffic through September. The hotel industry also reported a slowdown, with room occupancy declining. In 2009 worldwide tourism arrivals decreased by 3.8%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UNWTO_151-0"><a href="#cite_note-UNWTO-151">[151]</a></sup> By the first quarter of 2009, real travel demand in the United States had fallen 6% over six quarters. While this is considerably milder than what occurred after the <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">9/11 attacks</a>, the decline was at twice the rate, as real GDP has fallen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup>
</p><p>However, evidence suggests that tourism as a global phenomenon shows no signs of substantially abating in the long term.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> Many<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="This term requires quantification. (May 2020)">quantify</span></a></i>]</sup> people increasingly view vacations and travel as a necessity rather than a luxury, and this is reflected in tourist numbers recovering<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (May 2020)">when?</span></a></i>]</sup> some 6.6% globally over 2009, with growth up to 8% in emerging economies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UNWTO_151-1"><a href="#cite_note-UNWTO-151">[151]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Impacts_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic">Impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Tourism&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Impact_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_on_tourism" title="Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on tourism">Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on tourism</a></div>
<p>In 2020 the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a> lock-downs, travel bans and a substantial reduction in passenger travel by air and sea contributed to a <a href="/wiki/Impact_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic_on_tourism" title="Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on tourism">sharp decline in tourism activity</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup>
</p>

The majority of this footprint is exerted by and in high-income countries.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Nature+Climate+Change&amp;rft.atitle=The+carbon+footprint+of+global+tourism&amp;rft.volume=8&amp;rft.issue=6&amp;rft.pages=522-528&amp;rft.date=2018-05-07&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1038%2Fs41558-018-0141-x&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.semanticscholar.org%2FCorpusID%3A90810502%23id-name%3DS2CID&amp;rft.issn=1758-6798&amp;rft_id=info%3Abibcode%2F2018NatCC...8..522L&amp;rft.aulast=Lenzen&amp;rft.aufirst=Manfred&amp;rft.au=Sun%2C+Ya-Yen&amp;rft.au=Faturay%2C+Futu&amp;rft.au=Ting%2C+Yuan-Peng&amp;rft.au=Geschke%2C+Arne&amp;rft.au=Malik%2C+Arunima&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATourism"></span></span>

Retrieved <span class="nowrap">30 May</span> 2018</span>. <q>The globalisation of tourism has partially exacerbated the relationships of inequality and subservience that are so commonplace in host-guest encounters. <li id="cite_note-127"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-127">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Compare:
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation journal cs1" id="CITEREFGannonBaxterCollinsonCurran2017">Gannon, Martin Joseph; Baxter, Ian W.F.; Collinson, Elaine; Curran, Ross; Farrington, Thomas; Glasgow, Steven; Godsman, Elliot M.; Gori, Keith; Jack, Gordon R.A. (11 June 2017). <a class="external text" href="http://centaur.reading.ac.uk/70393/3/Umrah-SIJ-2017.pdf" rel="nofollow">"Travelling for Umrah: destination attributes, destination image, and post-travel intentions"</a> <span class="cs1-format">(PDF)</span>. <i>The Service Industries Journal</i>. <b>37</b> (7–8): 448–65. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doi_(identifier)" title="Doi (identifier)">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1080%2F02642069.2017.1333601" rel="nofollow">10.1080/02642069.2017.1333601</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISSN_(identifier)" title="ISSN (identifier)">ISSN</a> <a class="external text" href="//www.worldcat.org/issn/0264-2069" rel="nofollow">0264-2069</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S2CID_(identifier)" title="S2CID (identifier)">S2CID</a> <a class="external text" href="https://api.semanticscholar.org/CorpusID:54745153" rel="nofollow">54745153</a>. <q>The result from the structural model suggests that destination attributes influence perceived destination image. Further, such tourists are likely to revisit or recommend Islamic destinations if their experience matches their perceived image of the destination. This implies that, while the religious characteristics of the destination remain important, destination managers cannot disregard the tangential, non-religious attributes of a destination which are crucial in order to satisfy more conventional tourist desires.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=The+Service+Industries+Journal&amp;rft.atitle=Travelling+for+Umrah%3A+destination+attributes%2C+destination+image%2C+and+post-travel+intentions&amp;rft.volume=37&amp;rft.issue=7%E2%80%938&amp;rft.pages=448-65&amp;rft.date=2017-06-11&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.semanticscholar.org%2FCorpusID%3A54745153%23id-name%3DS2CID&amp;rft.issn=0264-2069&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1080%2F02642069.2017.1333601&amp;rft.aulast=Gannon&amp;rft.aufirst=Martin+Joseph&amp;rft.au=Baxter%2C+Ian+W.F.&amp;rft.au=Collinson%2C+Elaine&amp;rft.au=Curran%2C+Ross&amp;rft.au=Farrington%2C+Thomas&amp;rft.au=Glasgow%2C+Steven&amp;rft.au=Godsman%2C+Elliot+M.&amp;rft.au=Gori%2C+Keith&amp;rft.au=Jack%2C+Gordon+R.A.&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fcentaur.reading.ac.uk%2F70393%2F3%2FUmrah-SIJ-2017.pdf&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATourism"></span></span>
